{"answers": ["National Industrial Recovery Act", "NIRA"], "model_answer": "Based on the provided documents, the New Deal program that limited production in industry is the National Industrial Recovery Act (NIRA). NIRA was a program that aimed to stimulate economic recovery by promoting fair competition and reducing overproduction in industry. It established codes of fair competition and minimum wages, and prohibited child labor and excessive working hours. The program was implemented through the National Recovery Administration (NRA), which was established in 1933."}
